
The parity check matrix for W(3,23) minus a spread is a 24b x 
23b matrix, where b is 530.

The 1 coordinates of the first row of the circulants in the (q+1)xq rep matrix is \
given by Hrep.

The length of the code is 12190 and the check matrix has rank 
6625, so the full code has dimension 5565.

There is a generator matrix for the subcode of the form (P | id) where P is quasi \
cyclic 10b x 13b matrix, whose first rows are in the matrix Pbin.

The subcode has dimension 5300 so the rate is 0.4347826086956522.
